 Jinghu Hotel and Jinghu International Hotel are located at No. 1, Section 1, West Changjiang Road, Jingyang District, Deyang City, Sichuan Province. Covered by green trees and clustered with green flowers, Deyang Jinghu International Hotel stands on the bank of Jinghu Lake in the prime location of the city.
The hotel has a sufficient number of underground parking spaces, which are free for hotel guests.
It is very convenient to walk to the Confucian Temple and Food Street for about ten minutes.
